                    (a.first = 1
                      OR a.second = 1)
                    AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                        AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                  GROUP BY
                    a.attendance_dt

08-10-14 7:45 am	SELECT
                    AVG(totals.Total_Attendance) Avg_Total_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Total_Attendance) Max_Total_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Total_Attendance) Max_Total_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                  FROM (
                    SELECT
                      COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                      SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                    FROM
                      People p
                      INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                    WHERE
                      (a.first = 1
                        OR a.second = 1)
                      AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                            AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                    GROUP BY
                      a.attendance_dt
                  ) totals

                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Total_Attendance) Max_Total_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Total_Attendance) Max_Total_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                  FROM (
                    SELECT
                      COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                      SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                    FROM
                      People p
                      INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                    WHERE
                      (a.first = 1
                        OR a.second = 1)
                      AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                            AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                    GROUP BY
                      a.attendance_dt
                  ) totals

08-10-14 2:13 pm	SELECT
                    COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    DATE_FORMAT(attendance_dt,'%m/%d/%Y') Attendance_dt
                  FROM
                    People p
                    INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                  WHERE
                    (a.first = 1
                      OR a.second = 1)
                    AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                        AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                  GROUP BY
                    a.attendance_dt
                  ORDER BY
                    a.attendance_dt DESC

08-10-14 2:13 pm	SELECT
                    AVG(totals.Total_Attendance) Avg_Total_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Total_Attendance) Max_Total_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Total_Attendance) Min_Total_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                  FROM (
                    SELECT
                      COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                      SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                    FROM
                      People p
                      INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                    WHERE
                      (a.first = 1
                        OR a.second = 1)
                      AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                            AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                    GROUP BY
                      a.attendance_dt
                  ) totals

                    SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Adult_Attendance,

                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Kid_Attendance,

                    AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                        AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))

                    a.attendance_dt

08-10-14 2:20 pm	SELECT
                    AVG(totals.Total_Attendance) Avg_Total_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Total_Attendance) Max_Total_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Total_Attendance) Min_Total_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                  FROM (
                    SELECT
                      COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                      SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                    FROM
                      People p
                      INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                    WHERE
                      (a.first = 1
                        OR a.second = 1)
                      AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                            AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                    GROUP BY
                      a.attendance_dt
                  ) totals

                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Total_Attendance) Max_Total_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Total_Attendance) Min_Total_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                  FROM (
                    SELECT
                      COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                      SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                    FROM
                      People p
                      INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                    WHERE
                      (a.first = 1
                        OR a.second = 1)
                      AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                            AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                    GROUP BY
                      a.attendance_dt
                  ) totals

08-10-14 2:22 pm	SELECT
                    p.id,
                    CASE WHEN p.adult = 1 THEN 'true' ELSE 'false' END adult,
                    p.first_name,
                    p.last_name,
                    p.description,
                    COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance
                  FROM
                    People p
                    INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                  WHERE
                    (a.first = 1
                      OR a.second = 1)
                    AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                        AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                  GROUP BY
                    p.id
                  ORDER BY
                    Total_Attendance DESC,
                    p.description,
                    p.last_name,
                    p.first_name

08-12-14 4:46 pm	SELECT
                    p.id,
                    CASE WHEN p.adult = 1 THEN 'true' ELSE 'false' END adult,
                    p.first_name,
                    p.last_name,
                    p.description,
                    COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance
                  FROM
                    People p
                    INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                  WHERE
                    (a.first = 1
                      OR a.second = 1)
                    AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                        AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                  GROUP BY
                    p.id
                  ORDER BY
                    Total_Attendance DESC,
                    p.description,
                    p.last_name,
                    p.first_name

08-12-14 4:47 pm	SELECT
                    COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    DATE_FORMAT(attendance_dt,'%m/%d/%Y') Attendance_dt
                  FROM
                    People p
                    INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                  WHERE
                    (a.first = 1
                      OR a.second = 1)
                    AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                        AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                  GROUP BY
                    a.attendance_dt
                  ORDER BY
                    a.attendance_dt DESC

08-12-14 4:47 pm	SELECT
                    AVG(totals.Total_Attendance) Avg_Total_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Total_Attendance) Max_Total_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Total_Attendance) Min_Total_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                  FROM (
                    SELECT
                      COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                      SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                    FROM
                      People p
                      INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                    WHERE
                      (a.first = 1
                        OR a.second = 1)
                      AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                            AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                    GROUP BY
                      a.attendance_dt
                  ) totals

08-15-14 7:58 pm	SELECT
                    COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    DATE_FORMAT(attendance_dt,'%m/%d/%Y') Attendance_dt
                  FROM
                    People p
                    INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                  WHERE
                    (a.first = 1
                      OR a.second = 1)
                    AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                        AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                  GROUP BY
                    a.attendance_dt
                  ORDER BY
                    a.attendance_dt DESC

                    AVG(totals.Total_Attendance) Avg_Total_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Total_Attendance) Max_Total_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Total_Attendance) Min_Total_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                  FROM (
                    SELECT
                      COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                      SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                    FROM
                      People p
                      INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                    WHERE
                      (a.first = 1
                        OR a.second = 1)
                      AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                            AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                    GROUP BY
                      a.attendance_dt
                  ) totals

08-16-14 7:44 am	SELECT
                    COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    DATE_FORMAT(attendance_dt,'%m/%d/%Y') Attendance_dt
                  FROM
                    People p
                    INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                  WHERE
                    (a.first = 1
                      OR a.second = 1)
                    AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                        AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                  GROUP BY
                    a.attendance_dt
                  ORDER BY
                    a.attendance_dt DESC

08-16-14 7:44 am	SELECT
                    AVG(totals.Total_Attendance) Avg_Total_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Total_Attendance) Max_Total_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Total_Attendance) Min_Total_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                  FROM (
                    SELECT
                      COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                      SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                    FROM
                      People p
                      INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                    WHERE
                      (a.first = 1
                        OR a.second = 1)
                      AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                            AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                    GROUP BY
                      a.attendance_dt
                  ) totals

                      SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                    FROM
                      People p
                      INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                    WHERE
                      (a.first = 1
                        OR a.second = 1)
                      AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                            AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                    GROUP BY
                      a.attendance_dt
                  ) totals

08-18-14 9:16 pm	SELECT
                    COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    DATE_FORMAT(attendance_dt,'%m/%d/%Y') Attendance_dt
                  FROM
                    People p
                    INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                  WHERE
                    (a.first = 1
                      OR a.second = 1)
                    AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                        AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                  GROUP BY
                    a.attendance_dt
                  ORDER BY
                    a.attendance_dt DESC

08-18-14 9:16 pm	SELECT
                    AVG(totals.Total_Attendance) Avg_Total_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Total_Attendance) Max_Total_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Total_Attendance) Min_Total_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                  FROM (
                    SELECT
                      COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                      SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                    FROM
                      People p
                      INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                    WHERE
                      (a.first = 1
                        OR a.second = 1)
                      AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                            AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                    GROUP BY
                      a.attendance_dt
                  ) totals

08-18-14 9:17 pm	SELECT
                    p.id,
                    CASE WHEN p.adult = 1 THEN 'true' ELSE 'false' END adult,
                    p.first_name,
                    p.last_name,
                    p.description,
                    COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance
                  FROM
                    People p
                    INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                  WHERE
                    (a.first = 1
                      OR a.second = 1)
                    AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                        AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                  GROUP BY
                    p.id
                  ORDER BY
                    Total_Attendance DESC,
                    p.description,
                    p.last_name,
                    p.first_name

08-18-14 9:18 pm	SELECT
                    p.id,
                    CASE WHEN p.adult = 1 THEN 'true' ELSE 'false' END adult,
                    p.first_name,
                    p.last_name,
                    p.description,
                    COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance
                  FROM
                    People p
                    INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                  WHERE
                    (a.first = 1
                      OR a.second = 1)
                    AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                        AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                  GROUP BY
                    p.id
                  ORDER BY
                    Total_Attendance DESC,
                    p.description,
                    p.last_name,
                    p.first_name

                    p.id,
                    p.first_name,
                    p.last_name,

08-18-14 9:28 pm	SELECT
                    COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    DATE_FORMAT(attendance_dt,'%m/%d/%Y') Attendance_dt
                  FROM
                    People p
                    INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                  WHERE
                    (a.first = 1
                      OR a.second = 1)
                    AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                        AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                  GROUP BY
                    a.attendance_dt
                  ORDER BY
                    a.attendance_dt DESC

08-18-14 9:28 pm	SELECT
                    AVG(totals.Total_Attendance) Avg_Total_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Avg_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    AVG(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Avg_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Total_Attendance) Max_Total_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Max_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MAX(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Max_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Total_Attendance) Min_Total_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Adult_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Adult_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.First_Service_Kid_Attendance) Min_First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                    MIN(totals.Second_Service_Kid_Attendance) Min_Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                  FROM (
                    SELECT
                      COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                      SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=1 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Adult_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.first=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) First_Service_Kid_Attendance,
                      SUM(CASE WHEN p.adult=0 AND a.second=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) Second_Service_Kid_Attendance
                    FROM
                      People p
                      INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                    WHERE
                      (a.first = 1
                        OR a.second = 1)
                      AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                            AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                    GROUP BY
                      a.attendance_dt
                  ) totals

                    p.id,
                    CASE WHEN p.adult = 1 THEN 'true' ELSE 'false' END adult,
                    p.first_name,
                    p.last_name,
                    p.description,
                    COUNT(1) Total_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.first) First_Service_Attendance,
                    SUM(a.second) Second_Service_Attendance
                  FROM
                    People p
                    INNER JOIN Attendance a ON a.attended_by=p.id
                  WHERE
                    (a.first = 1
                      OR a.second = 1)
                    AND (a.attendance_dt >= STR_TO_DATE(:fromDate,'%m/%d/%Y')
                        AND a.attendance_dt <= STR_TO_DATE(:toDate,'%m/%d/%Y'))
                  GROUP BY
                    p.id
                  ORDER BY
                    Total_Attendance DESC,
                    p.description,
                    p.last_name,
                    p.first_name
